<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/rskgqd324/djy/blob/master/gb/21/7/1/n13061625.md#1" target="_blank">【百年透视】中共的经济谎言</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/rskgqd324/djy/blob/master/gb/21/7/1/n13061625.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/06/id13057325-0f8ddc95685b8b90f917f29fa47922b9-1-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>

<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/rskgqd324/djy/blob/master/gb/21/6/23/n13041339.md#1" target="_blank">盐让食物变美味 食盐、海盐、犹太盐怎么用？</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/rskgqd324/djy/blob/master/gb/21/6/23/n13041339.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/06/id13055342-shutterstock_659740363-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>如果你想要温和的盐味，犹太盐是最佳选择，而需要快速溶解时，最适合使用食盐，如用于烘焙食谱中。喜马拉雅盐的开采及特性都与食盐相似，除了含有一点铁与铜成分，使其带有粉红光泽及非常些微不同的风味。通常这种盐会比食盐颗粒更粗。犹太盐是一种粗粒盐，通常自盐矿床开采。海盐由海水蒸发后制成并含多种矿物质，如镁、钙、溴化物及自然生成的.........<br><img align="bottom" src="https://www.epochtimes.com/assets/themes/djy/images/time.gif"> 2021年06月30日 1:44 PM			</td></tr>
